                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Wednesday, September 3, 2014
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://i1211.photobucket.com/albums/cc435/bostonmerlin10/1%20May%202014%20and%20Onward/GlamPolishCBLChaosandCrocs109_zpsec0f0187.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="8772421345071441200" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="1492419239303514041" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="1492419239303514041">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     Falling Into Fall: Chaos &amp; Crocodiles Fireside Nights over Zoya Claire
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-1492419239303514041" itemprop="description articleBody">
                     Hi everyone! Today I have another fall-inspired mani to share with you. Last winter, I picked up
                     <b>
                      Chaos &amp; Crocodiles Fireside Nights
                     </b>
                     and I've been holding onto it
                     <span style="color: #4b4b4b;">
                      for
                     </span>
                     fall. The glitters are, of course, supposed to represent fire, but I think of falling leaves whenever I see this polish. I started off with a base of
                     <b>
                      Zoya Claire (from the new Entice Collection)
                     </b>
                     because I thought that the deep burgundy would really make the glitters pop. I used 2 coats of Fireside Nights over the base for this mani. Might I say, this glitter was so well behaved for a chunky glitter. It spread really well and smoothed out perfectly with 1 coat of a thicker topcoat and 1 coat of a quick-dry topcoat. Fireside Nights hasn't been restocked in the Chaos &amp; Crocodiles shop lately, but creator Sarey brings back older polishes from time-to-time, so it's always possible that it will make a reappearance.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://i1211.photobucket.com/albums/cc435/bostonmerlin10/1%20May%202014%20and%20Onward/GlamPolishCBLChaosandCrocs109_zpsec0f0187.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://i1211.photobucket.com/albums/cc435/bostonmerlin10/1%20May%202014%20and%20Onward/GlamPolishCBLChaosandCrocs109_zpsec0f0187.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <a name="more">
                     </a>
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://i1211.photobucket.com/albums/cc435/bostonmerlin10/1%20May%202014%20and%20Onward/GlamPolishCBLChaosandCrocs114_zps9ac8d5c5.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://i1211.photobucket.com/albums/cc435/bostonmerlin10/1%20May%202014%20and%20Onward/GlamPolishCBLChaosandCrocs114_zps9ac8d5c5.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://i1211.photobucket.com/albums/cc435/bostonmerlin10/1%20May%202014%20and%20Onward/GlamPolishCBLChaosandCrocs094_zpsfd3e6602.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="478" src="http://i1211.photobucket.com/albums/cc435/bostonmerlin10/1%20May%202014%20and%20Onward/GlamPolishCBLChaosandCrocs094_zpsfd3e6602.jpg" width="640"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                      <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                       <b style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px;">
                        Chaos &amp; Crocodiles
                       </b>
                       <span style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px;">
                        polishes
                       </span>
                       <span style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px;">
                        are available from their
                       </span>
                       <a href="http://chaosandcrocodiles.bigcartel.com/" style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px; text-decoration: none;">
                        Big Cartel shop
                       </a>
                       <span style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px;">
                        as well as from
                        <a href="http://meimeisignatures.com/index.php?id_category=392&amp;controller=category" style="text-decoration: none;">
                         Mei Mei's Signatures
                        </a>
                       </span>
                       <span style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px;">
                        <span style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px;">
                         and
                         <a href="http://www.norwaynails.com/collections/chaos-crocodiles">
                          Norway Nails
                         </a>
                         .
                        </span>
                        You can keep track of info on restocks and releases by following their
                       </span>
                       <a href="http://chaosandcrocodiles.blogspot.com/" style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px; text-decoration: none;">
                        blog
                       </a>
                       <span style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px;">
                        and
                       </span>
                       <a href="https://www.facebook.com/ChaosAndCrocodiles" style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px; text-decoration: none;">
                        Facebook
                       </a>
                       <span style="background-color: white; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px;">
                        .
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both;">
                      <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                       <span style="background-color: white; color: #4b4b4b; font-size: 15px; line-height: 20px;">
                       </span>
                       <b>
                        Zoya's Entice Collection
                       </b>
                       is now available for 
pre-order on
                       <a href="http://www.zoya.com/content/category/Zoya-Entice-Ignite-Fall-2014.html">
                        Zoya's website
                       </a>
                       (they
 retail for $9 each), and they will soon be available where Zoya is sold
 in your area (I always find them at Ulta locally).
                      </span>
                     </div>
